OBJECT Table 60000 Parking Header
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=22-04-15;
    Time=16:02:32;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    OnInsert=VAR
               ParkingSetup@1000 : Record 60005;
               ParkingLine@1001 : Record 60001;
               NoSeriesMgt@1002 : Codeunit 396;
               Error01@1004 : TextConst 'ENU=Parking lot is full';
               ParkingLots@1003 : Record 60004;
               ParkingHeader@1005 : Record 60000;
               Error02@1006 : TextConst 'ENU=Parking lot no. need to be selected';
               Error03@1007 : TextConst 'ENU=You can''t add another parking header for this customer';
               Error04@1008 : TextConst 'ENU=You can''t add another parking header for this parking lot';
               UserSetup@1009 : Record 91;
             BEGIN
               {
               ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("Customer No.","Customer No.");
               IF NOT ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                IF "Parking Lot No." = '' THEN BEGIN
                  ERROR(Error02);
                END ELSE BEGIN
                 ParkingLots.SETRANGE(ParkingLots."Parking lot No.","Parking Lot No.");
                 IF ParkingLots.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                  ParkingLots.CALCFIELDS("Occupied Parking Spaces");
                  IF ParkingLots."Occupied Parking Spaces" = ParkingLots."Parking Spaces" THEN
                   ERROR(Error01);
                 END;
                END;
               END ELSE BEGIN
                IF ParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" = TRUE THEN BEGIN
                 IF "Parking Lot No." = '' THEN BEGIN
                  ERROR(Error02);
                 END ELSE BEGIN
                  IF ParkingHeader."Parking Lot No." = "Parking Lot No." THEN
                    ERROR(Error04);
                  ParkingLots.SETRANGE(ParkingLots."Parking lot No.","Parking Lot No.");
                  IF ParkingLots.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                   ParkingLots.CALCFIELDS("Occupied Parking Spaces");
                   IF ParkingLots."Occupied Parking Spaces" = ParkingLots."Parking Spaces" THEN
                    ERROR(Error01);
                  END;
                 END;
                END ELSE BEGIN
                 ERROR(Error03);
               END;
               END;
               }

               IF "No." = '' THEN BEGIN
                 ParkingSetup.GET;
                 ParkingSetup.TESTFIELD("Parking Nos.");
                 NoSeriesMgt.InitSeries(ParkingSetup."Parking Nos.",xRec."No. Series",0D,"No.","No. Series");
               END;

               ParkingLine.INIT;
               ParkingLine."Parking Order No." := "No.";
               UserSetup.GET(USERID);
               ParkingLine."Parking Lot No." := UserSetup."Parking Lot No.";
               "Issued By" := UserSetup."User ID";
               ParkingLine."Entry Time" := CURRENTDATETIME;
               ParkingLots.SETRANGE(ParkingLots."Parking lot No.",UserSetup."Parking Lot No.");
               IF ParkingLots.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                ParkingLots.CALCFIELDS("Occupied Parking Spaces");
                IF ParkingLots."Occupied Parking Spaces" = ParkingLots."Parking Spaces" THEN
                 ERROR(Error01);
               END;
               ParkingLine.INSERT(TRUE);
             END;

    OnDelete=VAR
               ParkingLine@1000 : Record 60001;
               Confirmation@1001 : TextConst 'ENU=Parking lines have been deleted';
             BEGIN
               ParkingLine.SETFILTER("Parking Order No.",Rec."No.");
               IF ParkingLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                 ParkingLine.DELETEALL;
                 MESSAGE(Confirmation);
               END;
             END;

  }
  FIELDS
  {
    { 10  ;   ;No.                 ;Code20        ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   NotBlank=No }
    { 20  ;   ;Customer No.        ;Code20        ;TableRelation=Customer;
                                                   OnValidate=VAR
                                                                ParkingHeader@1000 : Record 60000;
                                                              BEGIN
                                                                //FillCustInfo("Customer No.");
                                                              END;

                                                   DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   NotBlank=No }
    { 30  ;   ;Issued By           ;Code50        ;TableRelation=User."User Name";
                                                   ValidateTableRelation=No;
                                                   TestTableRelation=No;
                                                   DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 40  ;   ;Total Amount        ;Decimal       ;FieldClass=FlowField;
                                                   CalcFormula=Sum("Parking Lines".Amount WHERE (Parking Order No.=FIELD(No.)));
                                                   Editable=No }
    { 50  ;   ;Total No. of Entries;Integer       ;FieldClass=FlowField;
                                                   CalcFormula=Count("Parking Lines" WHERE (Parking Order No.=FIELD(No.)));
                                                   Editable=Yes }
    { 60  ;   ;Document Date       ;DateTime      ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 70  ;   ;Posting Date        ;DateTime      ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 80  ;   ;Customer Name       ;Text100       ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 90  ;   ;Adress              ;Text100       ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 100 ;   ;Adress 2            ;Text50        ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 107 ;   ;No. Series          ;Code20        ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 110 ;   ;Post Code           ;Code20        ;TableRelation="Post Code";
                                                   DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 120 ;   ;City                ;Text30        ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 130 ;   ;Contract            ;Boolean       ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   Editable=No }
    { 140 ;   ;Accumulative Account;Boolean       ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   Editable=No }
    { 150 ;   ;Parking Lot No.     ;Code10        ;TableRelation="Parking Lots";
                                                   DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   NotBlank=No }
    { 160 ;   ;Customer Phone No.  ;Code20        ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 170 ;   ;Customer Email      ;Text40        ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
  }
  KEYS
  {
    {    ;No.                                     ;Clustered=Yes }
  }
  FIELDGROUPS
  {
  }
  CODE
  {
    VAR
      Customer@1000 : Record 18;
      Error0001@1003 : TextConst 'ENU=Entry Time cannot be greater than Departure Time';

    PROCEDURE FillCustInfo@1();
    VAR
      Contracts@1000 : Record 60006;
      Message000@1001 : TextConst 'ENU=This client''s monthly contract has expired. It will be charged at the one-time customer rate.';
      AccumulativeContracts@1002 : Record 60007;
    BEGIN
      Customer.GET("Customer No.");
      Contracts.SETRANGE("Customer No.",Customer."No.");
      IF (Contracts.FINDFIRST) AND (Contracts."Contract End Date" > CURRENTDATETIME) THEN
        Contract := TRUE
      ELSE IF (Contracts.FINDFIRST) AND (Contracts."Contract End Date" < CURRENTDATETIME) THEN
        MESSAGE(Message000);
      "Customer Name" := Customer.Name;
      Adress:= Customer.Address;
      "Adress 2" := Customer."Address 2";
      City := Customer.City;
      "Post Code" := Customer."Post Code";
      AccumulativeContracts.SETRANGE("Customer No.",Customer."No.");
      IF (AccumulativeContracts.FINDFIRST) THEN
        "Accumulative Account" := TRUE;
      "Customer Email" := Customer."E-Mail";
      "Customer Phone No." := Customer."Phone No.";
      "Document Date" := CURRENTDATETIME;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }
}

OBJECT Table 60001 Parking Lines
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=22-03-02;
    Time=10:46:50;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    OnInsert=VAR
               ParkingLots@1000 : Record 60004;
               Error01@1001 : TextConst 'ENU=Parking lot is full.';
               ParkingHeader@1002 : Record 60000;
               Error02@1003 : TextConst 'ENU=Only accumulative account can have more than one parking line.';
               ParkingLines@1004 : Record 60001;
               EmptyDateTime@1005 : DateTime;
               Error03@1006 : TextConst 'ENU=Car Plate No. can''t be blank.';
               UserSetup@1007 : Record 91;
               Cars@1008 : Record 60003;
             BEGIN
               UserSetup.GET(USERID);
               ParkingLots.SETRANGE(ParkingLots."Parking lot No.",UserSetup."Parking Lot No.");
               IF ParkingLots.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                ParkingLots.CALCFIELDS("Occupied Parking Spaces");
                IF ParkingLots."Occupied Parking Spaces" = ParkingLots."Parking Spaces" THEN
                 ERROR(Error01);
               END;
               ParkingHeader.SETRANGE(ParkingHeader."No.","Parking Order No.");
               IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                ParkingHeader.CALCFIELDS("Total No. of Entries");
                IF ParkingHeader."Total No. of Entries" >=1 THEN BEGIN
                 IF (ParkingHeader.Contract = TRUE) THEN
                  ERROR(Error02);
                 IF (ParkingHeader.Contract = FALSE) AND (ParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" = FALSE) THEN
                  ERROR(Error02);
                 IF (ParkingHeader.Contract = FALSE) AND (ParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" = TRUE) THEN BEGIN
                  ParkingLines.SETRANGE("Parking Order No.","Parking Order No.");
                  ParkingLines.SETFILTER("Departure Time",'=%1',EmptyDateTime);
                  IF ParkingLines.FINDFIRST THEN
                   ERROR(Error0002);
                 END;
                END;
               END;
               "Parking Lot No." := UserSetup."Parking Lot No.";
               {
               ParkingHeader.SETRANGE(ParkingHeader."No.", "Parking Order No.");
               IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                 "Customer No." := ParkingHeader."Customer No.";
                ParkingLots.SETRANGE(ParkingLots."Parking lot No.",ParkingHeader."Parking Lot No.");
                IF ParkingLots.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                 ParkingLots.CALCFIELDS("Occupied Parking Spaces");
                 IF ParkingLots."Occupied Parking Spaces" = ParkingLots."Parking Spaces" THEN BEGIN
                  ERROR(Error01);
                 END ELSE BEGIN
                  ParkingHeader.CALCFIELDS("Total No. of Entries");
                  IF ParkingHeader."Total No. of Entries" >=1 THEN BEGIN
                    IF (ParkingHeader.Contract = TRUE) THEN
                      ERROR(Error02);
                    IF (ParkingHeader.Contract = FALSE) AND (ParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" = FALSE) THEN
                      ERROR(Error02);
                    IF (ParkingHeader.Contract = FALSE) AND (ParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" = TRUE) THEN BEGIN
                     ParkingLines.SETRANGE("Parking Order No.","Parking Order No.");
                     ParkingLines.SETFILTER("Departure Time",'=%1',EmptyDateTime);
                     IF ParkingLines.FINDFIRST THEN
                      ERROR(Error0002);
                    END;
                  END;
                 END;
                END;
               END;
               }
               //"Parking Lot No.":= ParkingHeader."Parking Lot No.";
             END;

  }
  FIELDS
  {
    { 10  ;   ;Parking Order No.   ;Code20        ;TableRelation="Parking Header".No.;
                                                   DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 20  ;   ;Line No.            ;Integer       ;AutoIncrement=Yes;
                                                   DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 30  ;   ;Entry Time          ;DateTime      ;OnValidate=BEGIN
                                                                IF ("Entry Time" <> 0DT) AND ("Departure Time" <> 0DT) THEN BEGIN
                                                                  IF "Entry Time" > "Departure Time" THEN BEGIN
                                                                    ERROR(Error0001);
                                                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                   IF ("Departure Time" <> 0DT) AND ("Entry Time" <> 0DT) THEN
                                                                    "Duration (h)" := ("Departure Time" - "Entry Time")/3600000;
                                                                  END;
                                                                END;
                                                                IF "Duration (h)" <> 0 THEN
                                                                 CalculatePrices();
                                                              END;

                                                   DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   NotBlank=No }
    { 40  ;   ;Departure Time      ;DateTime      ;OnValidate=VAR
                                                                ParkingLots@1000 : Record 60004;
                                                                ParkingHeader@1001 : Record 60000;
                                                                Myrec@1002 : Record 60001;
                                                              BEGIN
                                                                IF ("Entry Time" <> 0DT) AND ("Departure Time" <> 0DT) THEN BEGIN
                                                                  IF "Entry Time" > "Departure Time" THEN BEGIN
                                                                    ERROR(Error0001);
                                                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                   IF ("Departure Time" <> 0DT) AND ("Entry Time" <> 0DT) THEN
                                                                    "Duration (h)" := ("Departure Time" - "Entry Time")/3600000;
                                                                  END;
                                                                END;
                                                                IF "Duration (h)" <> 0 THEN
                                                                 CalculatePrices();
                                                                Rec.MODIFY;
                                                                Myrec.SETRANGE("Parking Order No.",Rec."Parking Order No.");
                                                                Myrec.SETRANGE("Line No.",Rec."Line No.");
                                                                REPORT.RUNMODAL(60000,FALSE,FALSE,Myrec);
                                                                {
                                                                ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("No.","Parking Order No.");
                                                                IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                                                  IF ParkingHeader.Contract = TRUE THEN BEGIN
                                                                   ParkingHeader.DELETE;
                                                                   Rec.DELETE;
                                                                 END;
                                                                END;
                                                                }
                                                              END;

                                                   DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 50  ;   ;Duration (h)        ;Decimal       ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 60  ;   ;Car Plate No.       ;Code10        ;OnValidate=VAR
                                                                Cars@1000 : Record 60003;
                                                                Customer@1001 : Record 18;
                                                                ParkingHeader@1002 : Record 60000;
                                                                Error03@1003 : TextConst 'ENU=Cannot add another parking header for this customer in selected parking lot. Choose another parking lot or selected existing parking header.';
                                                                Error04@1004 : TextConst 'ENU=Cannot add another parking header for this customer.';
                                                                ParkingLines@1005 : Record 60001;
                                                                Error05@1006 : TextConst 'ENU=Cannot add another parking order for this until previuos is not closed.';
                                                                Error06@1007 : TextConst 'ENU=This customer already has an parking order for his accumulative account.';
                                                                Error07@1008 : TextConst 'ENU=This customer already has open parking order. Please close previuos one before creating new one.';
                                                                Error08@1009 : TextConst 'ENU=This car doesnt belong to this customer.';
                                                                Error09@1010 : TextConst 'ENU=Cannot choose this car, because it doesnt belong to this customer.';
                                                              BEGIN
                                                                Cars.SETRANGE("Car Plate No.",Rec."Car Plate No.");

                                                                ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("No.","Parking Order No.");
                                                                IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                                                 IF ParkingHeader."Customer No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                                                  IF Cars.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                                                   IF Cars."Customer No." <> ParkingHeader."Customer No." THEN
                                                                    ERROR(Error09);
                                                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                   ERROR(Error09);
                                                                  END;
                                                                 END;
                                                                END;

                                                                ParkingHeader.RESET;

                                                                IF Cars.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                                                 Customer.SETRANGE(Customer."No.",Cars."Customer No.");
                                                                 IF Customer.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                                                  ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("Customer No.",Customer."No.");
                                                                  IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                                                    IF ParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" <> TRUE THEN
                                                                     ERROR(Error07);
                                                                  END;
                                                                 END;
                                                                 ParkingHeader.RESET;
                                                                 ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("No.","Parking Order No.");
                                                                 IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                                                  ParkingHeader."Customer No." := Customer."No.";
                                                                  ParkingHeader.FillCustInfo();
                                                                  ParkingHeader.MODIFY;
                                                                 END;
                                                                END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                 ParkingHeader.RESET;
                                                                 ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("Customer No.",'A00008');
                                                                 IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                                                  REPEAT
                                                                   ParkingLines.SETRANGE("Parking Order No.",ParkingHeader."No.");
                                                                    IF ParkingLines.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                                                     REPEAT
                                                                      IF ParkingLines."Car Plate No." = "Car Plate No." THEN
                                                                       ERROR(Error05);
                                                                     UNTIL ParkingLines.NEXT <=0;
                                                                    END;
                                                                  UNTIL ParkingHeader.NEXT <= 0;
                                                                 END;
                                                                 ParkingHeader.RESET;
                                                                 ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("No.","Parking Order No.");
                                                                 IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                                                  ParkingHeader."Customer No." := 'A00008';
                                                                  ParkingHeader.FillCustInfo();
                                                                  ParkingHeader.MODIFY;
                                                                 END;
                                                                END;
                                                                {
                                                                ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("Customer No.","Customer No.");
                                                                IF NOT ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                                                 IF "Parking Lot No." = '' THEN BEGIN
                                                                   ERROR(Error02);
                                                                 END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                  ParkingLots.SETRANGE(ParkingLots."Parking lot No.","Parking Lot No.");
                                                                  IF ParkingLots.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                                                   ParkingLots.CALCFIELDS("Occupied Parking Spaces");
                                                                   IF ParkingLots."Occupied Parking Spaces" = ParkingLots."Parking Spaces" THEN
                                                                    ERROR(Error01);
                                                                  END;
                                                                 END;
                                                                END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                 IF ParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" = TRUE THEN BEGIN
                                                                  IF "Parking Lot No." = '' THEN BEGIN
                                                                   ERROR(Error02);
                                                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                   IF ParkingHeader."Parking Lot No." = "Parking Lot No." THEN
                                                                     ERROR(Error04);
                                                                   ParkingLots.SETRANGE(ParkingLots."Parking lot No.","Parking Lot No.");
                                                                   IF ParkingLots.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                                                    ParkingLots.CALCFIELDS("Occupied Parking Spaces");
                                                                    IF ParkingLots."Occupied Parking Spaces" = ParkingLots."Parking Spaces" THEN
                                                                     ERROR(Error01);
                                                                   END;
                                                                  END;
                                                                 END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                  ERROR(Error03);
                                                                END;
                                                                END;
                                                                }
                                                              END;

                                                   DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   NotBlank=No }
    { 70  ;   ;Amount              ;Decimal       ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 80  ;   ;Parking Lot No.     ;Code10        ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 90  ;   ;Customer No.        ;Code20        ;TableRelation=Customer;
                                                   OnValidate=VAR
                                                                ParkingHeader@1000 : Record 60000;
                                                              BEGIN
                                                                {
                                                                ParkingHeader.SETFILTER(ParkingHeader."Customer No.","Customer No.");
                                                                IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN
                                                                  ERROR('Record with this customer no already exists');
                                                                FillCustInfo("Customer No.");
                                                                }
                                                              END;

                                                   DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   NotBlank=Yes }
  }
  KEYS
  {
    {    ;Parking Order No.,Line No.              ;Clustered=Yes }
    {    ;Departure Time                           }
  }
  FIELDGROUPS
  {
  }
  CODE
  {
    VAR
      Error0001@1000 : TextConst 'ENU=Entry time cannot be greater than departure time';
      Cheque@1001 : Report 60000;
      Error0002@1002 : TextConst 'ENU=Can''t add another line until previuos one isn''t closed';

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalculatePrices@2();
    VAR
      ParkingHeader@1000 : Record 60000;
      ParkingPrices@1001 : Record 60002;
      Direction@1004 : Text;
      Precision@1003 : Decimal;
      Result@1002 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      Direction := '>';
      Precision := 0.01;
      ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("No.",Rec."Parking Order No.");
      ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST;
      IF (ParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" = TRUE) AND (ParkingHeader.Contract = FALSE) THEN BEGIN
       Amount := "Duration (h)" * 0.5;
       //Amount := ROUND(Result,Precision,Direction);
      END ELSE IF (ParkingHeader.Contract = TRUE) AND (ParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" = FALSE) THEN BEGIN
       Amount := 0;
      END ELSE IF (ParkingHeader.Contract = FALSE) AND (ParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" = FALSE) THEN BEGIN
       ParkingPrices.SETRANGE(ParkingPrices."Parking Lot No.","Parking Lot No.");
       ParkingPrices.SETFILTER("Amount of hours",'<=%1',"Duration (h)");
       ParkingPrices.SETCURRENTKEY("Amount of hours");
       ParkingPrices.SETASCENDING("Amount of hours",FALSE);
       IF ParkingPrices.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        Amount := "Duration (h)" * ParkingPrices.Rate;
        //Amount := ROUND(Result,Precision,Direction);
       END ELSE BEGIN
        Amount := "Duration (h)" * 2;
        //Amount := ROUND(Result,Precision,Direction);
       END;
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }
}

OBJECT Table 60003 Cars
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=22-03-01;
    Time=15:58:33;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    OnInsert=VAR
               Cars@1000 : Record 60003;
               Error01@1001 : TextConst 'ENU=A car with this number already exists';
               Error02@1002 : TextConst 'ENU=Cannot add more than 3 cars for one customer';
               NumberOfCars@1003 : Integer;
             BEGIN
               Cars.SETRANGE("Car Plate No.","Car Plate No.");
               IF Cars.FINDFIRST THEN
                 ERROR(Error01);
               Cars.RESET;
               Cars.SETRANGE("Customer No.","Customer No.");
               IF Cars.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                 NumberOfCars := Cars.COUNT;
                 IF NumberOfCars >= 3 THEN
                   ERROR(Error02);
               END;
             END;

  }
  FIELDS
  {
    { 10  ;   ;Car Plate No.       ;Code10        ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   NotBlank=Yes }

                                                   NotBlank=Yes }

OBJECT Table 60006 Contracts
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=22-03-01;
    Time=15:27:45;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    OnInsert=VAR
               Customer@1000 : Record 18;
               MessageContract@1001 : TextConst 'ENU=Contract can''t be created, because this customer has accumulative contract';
               ParkingSetup@1002 : Record 60005;
               NoSeriesMgt@1003 : Codeunit 396;
               ParkingHeader@1004 : Record 60000;
               Contracts@1005 : Record 60006;
               Error01@1006 : TextConst 'ENU=Contract with this customer number already exists';
               UserSetup@1007 : Record 91;
             BEGIN
               Contracts.SETRANGE(Contracts."Customer No.","Customer No.");
               IF NOT Contracts.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                Customer.SETRANGE("No.",Rec."Customer No.");
                IF Customer.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                 IF Customer."Accumulative Account" = TRUE THEN
                  ERROR(MessageContract);
                END;
               END ELSE BEGIN
                 ERROR(Error01);
               END;

               IF "Contract No." = '' THEN BEGIN
                 ParkingSetup.GET;
                 ParkingSetup.TESTFIELD("Contract Nos.");
                 NoSeriesMgt.InitSeries(ParkingSetup."Contract Nos.",xRec."No. Series",0D,"Contract No.","No. Series");
               END;

               "Document Date" := TODAY;
               UserSetup.GET(USERID);
               "Issued By" := UserSetup."User ID";
             END;

    OnDelete=VAR
               ParkingHeader@1000 : Record 60000;
               Customer@1001 : Record 18;
             BEGIN
               Customer.SETRANGE("No.",Rec."Customer No.");
               IF Customer.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                Customer.Contract := FALSE;
                Customer.MODIFY;
                ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("Customer No.",Rec."Customer No.");
                 IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                  ParkingHeader.Contract := FALSE;
                  ParkingHeader.MODIFY;
                 END;
               END;
             END;

  }
  FIELDS
  {
    { 10  ;   ;Contract No.        ;Code20        ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   NotBlank=No }
    { 20  ;   ;Customer No.        ;Code20        ;TableRelation=Customer;
                                                   OnValidate=BEGIN
                                                                FillCustomerInfo("Customer No.");
                                                              END;

                                                   DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   NotBlank=Yes }
    { 30  ;   ;Customer Name       ;Text100       ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 40  ;   ;Document Date       ;Date          ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 50  ;   ;Contract Start Date ;DateTime      ;OnValidate=VAR
                                                                Error0001@1000 : TextConst 'ENU=Contract start date can''t be higher than contract end date';
                                                                Myrec@1001 : Record 60006;
                                                                ContractsCodeUnit@1002 : Codeunit 60002;
                                                              BEGIN
                                                                CountContractEndDate("Contract Start Date");
                                                                "Document Date" := DT2DATE("Contract Start Date");
                                                                Amount := 60;
                                                                "Remaining Amount" := 60;
                                                                Rec.MODIFY;
                                                                Myrec.SETRANGE("Contract No.",Rec."Contract No.");
                                                                Myrec.SETRANGE("Customer No.",Rec."Customer No.");
                                                                REPORT.RUNMODAL(60003,FALSE,FALSE,Myrec);
                                                                ContractsCodeUnit.PostContractOrder(Rec);
                                                              END;

                                                   DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   NotBlank=Yes }
    { 60  ;   ;Contract End Date   ;DateTime      ;OnValidate=VAR
                                                                Error0001@1000 : TextConst 'ENU=Contract start date can''t be higher than contract end date';
                                                              BEGIN
                                                              END;

                                                   DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 70  ;   ;Issued By           ;Code50        ;TableRelation=User."User Name";
                                                   ValidateTableRelation=No;
                                                   TestTableRelation=No;
                                                   DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   NotBlank=Yes }
    { 80  ;   ;Amount              ;Decimal       ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   Editable=No }
    { 90  ;   ;Remaining Amount    ;Decimal       ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   Editable=No }
    { 107 ;   ;No. Series          ;Code20        ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
  }
  KEYS
  {
    {    ;Contract No.,Customer No.               ;Clustered=Yes }
  }
  FIELDGROUPS

    LOCAL PROCEDURE FillCustomerInfo@1("Customer No."@1000 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      Customer@1001 : Record 18;
    BEGIN
      Customer.GET("Customer No.");
      "Customer Name" := Customer.Name;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CountContractEndDate@2(ContractStartDate@1000 : DateTime);
    VAR
      Date@1001 : Date;
      Time@1002 : Time;
      NewDateTime@1003 : DateTime;
    BEGIN
      Time := DT2TIME(ContractStartDate);
      Date := DT2DATE(ContractStartDate);
      Date += 30;
      NewDateTime := CREATEDATETIME(Date,Time);
      "Contract End Date" := NewDateTime;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

OBJECT Table 60007 Accumulative Savings Contracts
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=21-12-27;
    Time=18:24:15;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    OnInsert=VAR
               Customer@1000 : Record 18;
               MessageContract@1001 : TextConst 'ENU=Accumulative contract can''t be created, because this customer has monthly contract';
               ParkingSetup@1003 : Record 60005;
               NoSeriesMgt@1002 : Codeunit 396;
               ParkingHeader@1004 : Record 60000;
               AccumulativeAccounts@1005 : Record 60007;
               Error01@1006 : TextConst 'ENU=An account already exists with this customer number';
             BEGIN
               AccumulativeAccounts.SETRANGE(AccumulativeAccounts."Customer No.","Customer No.");
               IF NOT AccumulativeAccounts.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                Customer.SETRANGE("No.",Rec."Customer No.");
                IF Customer.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                 IF Customer.Contract = TRUE THEN BEGIN
                  ERROR(MessageContract);
                 END ELSE BEGIN
                  Customer."Accumulative Account" := TRUE;
                  Customer.MODIFY;
                  ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("Customer No.",Rec."Customer No.");
                  IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                   ParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" := TRUE;
                   ParkingHeader.MODIFY;
                  END;
                 END;
                END;
               END ELSE BEGIN
                 ERROR(Error01);
               END;

               IF "Accumulative Account No." = '' THEN BEGIN
                 ParkingSetup.GET;
                 ParkingSetup.TESTFIELD("Accumulative Contract Nos.");
                 NoSeriesMgt.InitSeries(ParkingSetup."Accumulative Contract Nos.",xRec."No. Series",0D,"Accumulative Account No.","No. Series");
               END;
             END;

    OnDelete=VAR
               Customer@1000 : Record 18;
               ParkingHeader@1001 : Record 60000;
             BEGIN
               Customer.SETRANGE("No.",Rec."Customer No.");
               IF Customer.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                Customer."Accumulative Account" := FALSE;
                Customer.MODIFY;
                ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("Customer No.",Rec."Customer No.");
                 IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                  ParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" := FALSE;
                  ParkingHeader.MODIFY;
                 END;
               END;
             END;

  }
  FIELDS
  {
    { 10  ;   ;Accumulative Account No.;Code20    ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   NotBlank=No }
    { 20  ;   ;Customer No.        ;Code20        ;TableRelation=Customer;
                                                   OnValidate=BEGIN
                                                                FillCustomerInfo("Customer No.");
                                                              END;

                                                   DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   NotBlank=Yes }
    { 30  ;   ;Customer Name       ;Text100       ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 40  ;   ;Document Date       ;Date          ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
    { 50  ;   ;Contract Start Date ;Date          ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   NotBlank=Yes }
    { 60  ;   ;Issued By           ;Code50        ;TableRelation=User."User Name";
                                                   ValidateTableRelation=No;
                                                   TestTableRelation=No;
                                                   DataClassification=ToBeClassified;
                                                   NotBlank=Yes }
    { 107 ;   ;No. Series          ;Code20        ;DataClassification=ToBeClassified }
  }
  KEYS
  {
    {    ;Accumulative Account No.,Customer No.   ;Clustered=Yes }
  }
  FIELDGROUPS
  {
  }
  CODE
  {

      Customer@1001 : Record 18;

      "Customer Name" := Customer.Name;

OBJECT Report 60000 Cheque

                  ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("No.","Parking Lines"."Parking Order No.");
                  IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                    IF ParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" = TRUE THEN
                      IsAccumulative := TRUE;
                    IF ParkingHeader.Contract = TRUE THEN
                      IsContract := TRUE;
                    IF (ParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" = FALSE) AND (ParkingHeader.Contract = FALSE) THEN
                      IsShortTerm := TRUE;
                  END;
                END;

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               REPEAT
                                 TotalDuration := "Posted Parking Lines"."Duration (h)" + TotalDuration;
                               UNTIL "Posted Parking Lines".NEXT = 0;
                               EVALUATE(Dur,FORMAT(ROUND(TotalDuration,0.1)));

                             END;

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

OBJECT Report 60005 Monthly report
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=22-04-19;
    Time=12:43:22;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    OnPreReport=VAR
                  UserSetup@1000 : Record 91;
                  Time@1001 : Time;
                  Date@1002 : Date;
                  Time1@1003 : Time;
                  Date1@1004 : Integer;
                  NewDateTime@1005 : DateTime;
                BEGIN
                  UserSetup.GET(USERID);
                  UserName := UserSetup."User ID";
                  Company := COMPANYNAME;
                  IF (StartDate = 0DT) AND (EndDate = 0DT) THEN BEGIN
                    NewDateTime := CURRENTDATETIME;
                    Time := DT2TIME(NewDateTime);
                    Date := DT2DATE(NewDateTime);
                    Date -= 30;
                    NewDateTime := CREATEDATETIME(Date,Time);
                    StartDate:= NewDateTime;
                    EndDate := CURRENTDATETIME;
                  END;
                  IF Type = Type::MonthlyContract THEN BEGIN
                    ShowSubscriptionTablix := TRUE;
                    ShowShortTimeTablix := FALSE;
                    ShowCummulativeAccountsTablix := FALSE;
                  END ELSE IF Type = Type::Accumulative THEN BEGIN
                    ShowCummulativeAccountsTablix := TRUE;
                    ShowShortTimeTablix := FALSE;
                    ShowSubscriptionTablix := FALSE;
                  END ELSE BEGIN
                    ShowShortTimeTablix := TRUE;
                    ShowSubscriptionTablix := FALSE;
                    ShowCummulativeAccountsTablix := FALSE
                  END;
                END;

  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

OBJECT Codeunit 60000 ParkingOrderPost
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=22-04-15;
    Time=14:00:02;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    OnRun=BEGIN
          END;

  }
  CODE
  {
    VAR
      NextLineNo@1000 : Integer;
      NextEntryNo@1001 : Integer;
      PostedParkingHeader@1002 : Record 60008;

    PROCEDURE PostOrder@1(ParkingOrder@1000 : Record 60000) : Code[20];
    VAR
      ParkingLines@1001 : Record 60001;
      PostedParkingLines@1003 : Record 60009;
      ParkingJournalLine@1004 : Record 60010;
    BEGIN
      ParkingOrder.CALCFIELDS("Total Amount","Total No. of Entries");
      ParkingLines.SETRANGE("Parking Order No.",ParkingOrder."No.");
      PostedParkingHeader.INIT;
      PostedParkingHeader."Customer No." := ParkingOrder."Customer No.";
      PostedParkingHeader."Issued By" := ParkingOrder."Issued By";
      PostedParkingHeader."Document Date" := ParkingOrder."Document Date";
      PostedParkingHeader."Posting Date" := ParkingOrder."Posting Date";
      PostedParkingHeader."Customer Name":= ParkingOrder."Customer Name";
      PostedParkingHeader.Adress := ParkingOrder.Adress;
      PostedParkingHeader."Adress 2" := ParkingOrder."Adress 2";
      PostedParkingHeader."Post Code" := ParkingOrder."Post Code";
      PostedParkingHeader.City := ParkingOrder.City;
      PostedParkingHeader.Contract := ParkingOrder.Contract;
      PostedParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" := ParkingOrder."Accumulative Account";
      PostedParkingHeader."Total Amount" := ParkingOrder."Total Amount";
      PostedParkingHeader."Total No. of Entries" := ParkingOrder."Total No. of Entries";
      PostedParkingHeader."Customer Email" := ParkingOrder."Customer Email";
      PostedParkingHeader."Customer Phone No." := ParkingOrder."Customer Phone No.";
      PostedParkingHeader."Remaining Amount" := ParkingOrder."Total Amount";
      IF PostedParkingHeader.INSERT(TRUE) THEN BEGIN
        //MESSAGE('Posted Rental Header is listed');
        ParkingOrder.DELETE;
      END;
      IF ParkingLines.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
       REPEAT
        IF NOT ParkingOrder.Contract = TRUE THEN BEGIN
        ParkingJournalLine.INIT;
        LineNo();
        ParkingJournalLine."Line No." := NextLineNo;
        ParkingJournalLine."Entry Time" := ParkingLines."Entry Time";
        ParkingJournalLine."Departure Time" := ParkingLines."Departure Time";
        ParkingJournalLine."Duration (h)" := ParkingLines."Duration (h)";
        ParkingJournalLine."Car Plate No." := ParkingLines."Car Plate No.";
        ParkingJournalLine.Amount := ParkingLines.Amount;
        ParkingJournalLine."Parking Lot No." := ParkingLines."Parking Lot No.";
        ParkingJournalLine."Customer No." := ParkingLines."Customer No.";
        ParkingJournalLine."Actual Date of Entry" := TODAY;
        ParkingJournalLine."Document No." := PostedParkingHeader."No.";
        ParkingJournalLine."Entry Type" := ParkingJournalLine."Entry Type"::Order;
        ParkingJournalLine.INSERT;
        END;
        PostedParkingLines.INIT;
        PostedParkingLines."Parking Order No." := PostedParkingHeader."No.";
        PostedParkingLines."Line No." := ParkingLines."Line No.";
        PostedParkingLines."Entry Time" := ParkingLines."Entry Time";
        PostedParkingLines."Departure Time" := ParkingLines."Departure Time";
        PostedParkingLines."Duration (h)" := ParkingLines."Duration (h)";
        PostedParkingLines."Car Plate No." := ParkingLines."Car Plate No.";
        PostedParkingLines.Amount := ParkingLines.Amount;
        PostedParkingLines."Parking Lot No." := ParkingLines."Parking Lot No.";
        //PostedParkingLines."Customer No." := ParkingLines."Customer No.";
        PostedParkingLines."Entry Type" := PostedParkingLines."Entry Type"::Order;
        PostedParkingLines.INSERT;
       UNTIL ParkingLines.NEXT = 0;
       ParkingLines.DELETE;
      END;
      IF NOT ParkingOrder.Contract = TRUE THEN
       PostJournalToLedger(PostedParkingHeader."No.");
      EXIT(PostedParkingHeader."No.");
    END;

    PROCEDURE PostJournalToLedger@3("Order No"@1000 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      ParkingJournalLine@1001 : Record 60010;
      ParkingLedgerEntry@1002 : Record 60011;
    BEGIN
      ParkingJournalLine.SETRANGE("Document No.","Order No");
      IF ParkingJournalLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD("Document No.");
          //ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD("Customer No.");
          ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD("Parking Lot No.");
          ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD(Amount);
          ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD("Car Plate No.");
          ParkingLedgerEntry.INIT;
          EntryNumber();
          ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry No." := NextEntryNo;
          ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry Time" := ParkingJournalLine."Entry Time";
          ParkingLedgerEntry."Departure Time" := ParkingJournalLine."Departure Time";
          ParkingLedgerEntry."Duration (h)" := ParkingJournalLine."Duration (h)";
          ParkingLedgerEntry."Car Plate No." := ParkingJournalLine."Car Plate No.";
          ParkingLedgerEntry.Amount := ParkingJournalLine.Amount;
          ParkingLedgerEntry."Parking Lot No." := ParkingJournalLine."Parking Lot No.";
          ParkingLedgerEntry."Customer No." := PostedParkingHeader."Customer No.";
          ParkingLedgerEntry."Actual Date of Entry" := TODAY;
          ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry Type" := ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry Type"::Order;
          ParkingLedgerEntry."Document No." := ParkingJournalLine."Document No.";
          IF ParkingLedgerEntry.INSERT THEN BEGIN
            //MESSAGE('Parking Ledger Entry Posted');
            ParkingJournalLine.DELETE;
          END;
        UNTIL ParkingJournalLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      MESSAGE('Posting done');
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckOrder@2(ParkingOrder@1000 : Record 60000) Check : Boolean;
    VAR
      ParkingLines@1001 : Record 60001;
    BEGIN
      Check := FALSE;
      ParkingOrder.TESTFIELD("Customer No.");
      ParkingOrder.TESTFIELD("Customer Name");
      ParkingOrder.TESTFIELD("Posting Date");
      ParkingOrder.TESTFIELD("Document Date");
      ParkingLines.SETRANGE("Parking Order No.",ParkingOrder."No.");
      IF ParkingLines.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          ParkingLines.TESTFIELD("Parking Order No.");
          ParkingLines.TESTFIELD("Entry Time");
          ParkingLines.TESTFIELD("Departure Time");
          ParkingLines.TESTFIELD("Car Plate No.");
          ParkingLines.TESTFIELD("Duration (h)");
        UNTIL ParkingLines.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      Check := TRUE;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE LineNo@4();
    VAR
      ParkingJournalLine@1000 : Record 60010;
    BEGIN
      IF ParkingJournalLine.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
       NextLineNo := ParkingJournalLine."Line No." + 1;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        NextLineNo := 1;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE EntryNumber@5();
    VAR
      ParkingLedgerEntry@1000 : Record 60011;
    BEGIN
      IF ParkingLedgerEntry.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
        NextEntryNo := ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry No." + 1;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        NextEntryNo := 1;
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }
}

OBJECT Codeunit 60001 Payment Post
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=22-02-17;
    Time=14:51:17;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    OnRun=BEGIN
          END;

  }
  CODE
  {
    VAR
      NextLineNo@1001 : Integer;
      NextEntryNo@1000 : Integer;

    PROCEDURE PostPayment@1(PostedParkingHeader@1000 : Record 60008;PaymentSum@1003 : Decimal);
    VAR
      PostedParkingLines@1002 : Record 60009;
      ParkingJournalLine@1001 : Record 60010;
      ParkingLedgerEntry@1004 : Record 60011;
    BEGIN
      IF PaymentSum > 0 THEN
       PaymentSum := PaymentSum * -1;

      ParkingJournalLine.INIT;
      LineNo();
      ParkingJournalLine."Line No." := NextLineNo;
      //ParkingJournalLine."Entry Time" := ParkingLines."Entry Time";
      //ParkingJournalLine."Departure Time" := ParkingLines."Departure Time";
      //ParkingJournalLine."Duration (h)" := PostedParkingLines."Duration (h)";
      //ParkingJournalLine."Car Plate No." := PostedParkingLines."Car Plate No.";
      ParkingJournalLine.Amount := PaymentSum;
      //ParkingJournalLine."Parking Lot No." := PostedParkingLines."Parking Lot No.";
      ParkingJournalLine."Customer No." := PostedParkingHeader."Customer No.";
      ParkingJournalLine."Actual Date of Entry" := TODAY;
      ParkingJournalLine."Document No." := PostedParkingHeader."No.";
      ParkingJournalLine."Entry Type" := ParkingJournalLine."Entry Type"::Payment;
      ParkingJournalLine.INSERT;

      ParkingJournalLine.SETRANGE("Document No.",PostedParkingHeader."No.");
      IF ParkingJournalLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
       ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD("Document No.");
       ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD("Customer No.");
       //ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD("Parking Lot No.");
       ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD(Amount);
       //ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD("Car Plate No.");
       ParkingLedgerEntry.INIT;
       EntryNumber();
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry No." := NextEntryNo;
       //ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry Time" := ParkingJournalLine."Entry Time";
       //ParkingLedgerEntry."Departure Time" := ParkingJournalLine."Departure Time";
       //ParkingLedgerEntry."Duration (h)" := ParkingJournalLine."Duration (h)";
       //ParkingLedgerEntry."Car Plate No." := ParkingJournalLine."Car Plate No.";
       ParkingLedgerEntry.Amount := ParkingJournalLine.Amount;
       //ParkingLedgerEntry."Parking Lot No." := ParkingJournalLine."Parking Lot No.";
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Customer No." := ParkingJournalLine."Customer No.";
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Actual Date of Entry" := TODAY;
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry Type" := ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry Type"::Payment;
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Document No." := ParkingJournalLine."Document No.";
       IF ParkingLedgerEntry.INSERT THEN BEGIN
        //MESSAGE('Parking Ledger Payment Entry Posted');
        ParkingJournalLine.DELETE;
       END;
       PostedParkingHeader.SETRANGE("No.",ParkingLedgerEntry."Document No.");
      {
       IF PostedParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        PostedParkingHeader."Total Amount" := PostedParkingHeader."Total Amount" + PaymentSum;
        PostedParkingHeader.MODIFY;
       END;
       }
       MESSAGE('Payment done');
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE LineNo@2();
    VAR
      ParkingJournalLine@1000 : Record 60010;
    BEGIN
      IF ParkingJournalLine.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
       NextLineNo := ParkingJournalLine."Line No." + 1;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        NextLineNo := 1;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE EntryNumber@3();
    VAR
      ParkingLedgerEntry@1000 : Record 60011;
    BEGIN
      IF ParkingLedgerEntry.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
        NextEntryNo := ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry No." + 1;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        NextEntryNo := 1;
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }
}

  {
    VAR
      NextLineNo@1001 : Integer;
      NextEntryNo@1000 : Integer;

    PROCEDURE PostContractPayment@1(Contract@1000 : Record 60006;PaymentSum@1003 : Decimal);
    VAR
      PostedParkingLines@1002 : Record 60009;
      ParkingJournalLine@1001 : Record 60010;
      ParkingLedgerEntry@1004 : Record 60011;
    BEGIN
      IF PaymentSum > 0 THEN
       PaymentSum := PaymentSum * -1;

      ParkingJournalLine.INIT;
      LineNo();
      ParkingJournalLine."Line No." := NextLineNo;
      ParkingJournalLine.Amount := PaymentSum;
      ParkingJournalLine."Customer No." := Contract."Customer No.";
      ParkingJournalLine."Actual Date of Entry" := TODAY;
      ParkingJournalLine."Document No." := Contract."Contract No.";
      ParkingJournalLine."Entry Type" := ParkingJournalLine."Entry Type"::ContractPayment;
      ParkingJournalLine.INSERT;

      ParkingJournalLine.SETRANGE("Document No.",Contract."Contract No.");
      IF ParkingJournalLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
       ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD("Document No.");
       ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD("Customer No.");
       ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD(Amount);
       ParkingLedgerEntry.INIT;
       EntryNumber();
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry No." := NextEntryNo;
       ParkingLedgerEntry.Amount := ParkingJournalLine.Amount;
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Customer No." := ParkingJournalLine."Customer No.";
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Actual Date of Entry" := TODAY;
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry Type" := ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry Type"::ContractPayment;
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Document No." := ParkingJournalLine."Document No.";
       IF ParkingLedgerEntry.INSERT THEN BEGIN
        //MESSAGE('Parking Ledger Payment Entry Posted');
        ParkingJournalLine.DELETE;
       END;
       Contract.SETRANGE("Contract No.",ParkingLedgerEntry."Document No.");
       IF Contract.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        Contract."Remaining Amount" := Contract."Remaining Amount" + PaymentSum;
        Contract.MODIFY;
        MESSAGE('Payment done');
       END;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE LineNo@2();
    VAR
      ParkingJournalLine@1000 : Record 60010;
    BEGIN
      IF ParkingJournalLine.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
       NextLineNo := ParkingJournalLine."Line No." + 1;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        NextLineNo := 1;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE EntryNumber@3();
    VAR
      ParkingLedgerEntry@1000 : Record 60011;
    BEGIN
      IF ParkingLedgerEntry.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
        NextEntryNo := ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry No." + 1;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        NextEntryNo := 1;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE PostContractOrder@4(Contract@1000 : Record 60006);
    VAR
      PostedParkingLines@1002 : Record 60009;
      ParkingJournalLine@1001 : Record 60010;
      ParkingLedgerEntry@1004 : Record 60011;
    BEGIN
      ParkingJournalLine.INIT;
      LineNo();
      ParkingJournalLine."Line No." := NextLineNo;
      ParkingJournalLine.Amount := Contract."Remaining Amount";
      ParkingJournalLine."Customer No." := Contract."Customer No.";
      ParkingJournalLine."Actual Date of Entry" := TODAY;
      ParkingJournalLine."Document No." := Contract."Contract No.";
      ParkingJournalLine."Entry Type" := ParkingJournalLine."Entry Type"::ContractOrder;
      ParkingJournalLine.INSERT;

      ParkingJournalLine.SETRANGE("Document No.",Contract."Contract No.");
      IF ParkingJournalLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
       ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD("Document No.");
       ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD("Customer No.");
       ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD(Amount);
       ParkingLedgerEntry.INIT;
       EntryNumber();
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry No." := NextEntryNo;
       ParkingLedgerEntry.Amount := ParkingJournalLine.Amount;
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Customer No." := ParkingJournalLine."Customer No.";
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Actual Date of Entry" := TODAY;
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry Type" := ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry Type"::ContractOrder;
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Document No." := ParkingJournalLine."Document No.";
       IF ParkingLedgerEntry.INSERT THEN BEGIN
        MESSAGE('Parking Ledger Order Entry Posted');
        ParkingJournalLine.DELETE;
       END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE ExtendContract@5(Contract@1000 : Record 60006;PaymentSum@1003 : Decimal);
    VAR
      PostedParkingLines@1002 : Record 60009;
      ParkingJournalLine@1001 : Record 60010;
      ParkingLedgerEntry@1004 : Record 60011;
      NewDate@1007 : Date;
      NewTime@1006 : Time;
      NewDateTime@1005 : DateTime;
      NewEndTime@1008 : DateTime;
    BEGIN
      IF PaymentSum > 0 THEN
       PaymentSum := PaymentSum * -1;

      ParkingJournalLine.INIT;
      LineNo();
      ParkingJournalLine."Line No." := NextLineNo;
      ParkingJournalLine.Amount := PaymentSum;
      ParkingJournalLine."Customer No." := Contract."Customer No.";
      ParkingJournalLine."Actual Date of Entry" := TODAY;
      ParkingJournalLine."Document No." := Contract."Contract No.";
      ParkingJournalLine."Entry Type" := ParkingJournalLine."Entry Type"::ContractPayment;
      ParkingJournalLine.INSERT;

      ParkingJournalLine.SETRANGE("Document No.",Contract."Contract No.");
      IF ParkingJournalLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
       ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD("Document No.");
       ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD("Customer No.");
       ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD(Amount);
       ParkingLedgerEntry.INIT;
       EntryNumber();
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry No." := NextEntryNo;
       ParkingLedgerEntry.Amount := ParkingJournalLine.Amount;
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Customer No." := ParkingJournalLine."Customer No.";
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Actual Date of Entry" := TODAY;
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry Type" := ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry Type"::ContractPayment;
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Document No." := ParkingJournalLine."Document No.";
       IF ParkingLedgerEntry.INSERT THEN BEGIN
        //MESSAGE('Parking Ledger Payment Entry Posted');
        ParkingJournalLine.DELETE;
       END;
      END;
      MESSAGE('Payment done');
      Contract.SETRANGE("Contract No.",ParkingLedgerEntry."Document No.");
      IF Contract.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
       Contract.Amount := Contract.Amount - PaymentSum;
       Contract."Remaining Amount" := Contract."Remaining Amount" - PaymentSum;
      END;
      NewDateTime := CREATEDATETIME(TODAY, TIME);
      NewTime := DT2TIME(NewDateTime);
      NewDate := DT2DATE(NewDateTime);
      NewDate += 30;
      NewEndTime := CREATEDATETIME(NewDate,NewTime);
      Contract."Contract End Date" := NewEndTime;
      Contract.MODIFY;
      REPORT.RUNMODAL(60003,FALSE,FALSE,Contract);
      Contract."Remaining Amount" := Contract."Remaining Amount" + PaymentSum;
      Contract.MODIFY;
    END;

    PROCEDURE PostExtendedContract@6(Contract@1000 : Record 60006;PaymentSum@1003 : Decimal);
    VAR
      PostedParkingLines@1002 : Record 60009;
      ParkingJournalLine@1001 : Record 60010;
      ParkingLedgerEntry@1004 : Record 60011;
    BEGIN
      //Contract."Remaining Amount" := Contract."Remaining Amount" + PaymentSum;
      //Contract.MODIFY;
      ParkingJournalLine.INIT;
      LineNo();
      ParkingJournalLine."Line No." := NextLineNo;
      ParkingJournalLine.Amount := PaymentSum;
      ParkingJournalLine."Customer No." := Contract."Customer No.";
      ParkingJournalLine."Actual Date of Entry" := TODAY;
      ParkingJournalLine."Document No." := Contract."Contract No.";
      ParkingJournalLine."Entry Type" := ParkingJournalLine."Entry Type"::ContractOrder;
      ParkingJournalLine.INSERT;

      ParkingJournalLine.SETRANGE("Document No.",Contract."Contract No.");
      IF ParkingJournalLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
       ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD("Document No.");
       ParkingJournalLine.TESTFIELD("Customer No.");
       ParkingLedgerEntry.INIT;
       EntryNumber();
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry No." := NextEntryNo;
       ParkingLedgerEntry.Amount := ParkingJournalLine.Amount;
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Customer No." := ParkingJournalLine."Customer No.";
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Actual Date of Entry" := TODAY;
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry Type" := ParkingLedgerEntry."Entry Type"::ContractOrder;
       ParkingLedgerEntry."Document No." := ParkingJournalLine."Document No.";
       IF ParkingLedgerEntry.INSERT THEN BEGIN
        //MESSAGE('Parking Ledger Order Entry Posted');
        ParkingJournalLine.DELETE;
       END;
      END;
      ExtendContract(Contract,PaymentSum);
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }
}

OBJECT Codeunit 60004 CarRegistration
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=22-02-17;
    Time=11:27:58;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    OnRun=VAR
            CarPlateNo@1000 : Code[10];
            ParkingLines@1001 : Record 60001;
            Cars@1002 : Record 60003;
            ParkingHeader@1003 : Record 60000;
            UserSetup@1004 : Record 91;
            ParkingOrder@1005 : Page 60000;
            Error000@1006 : TextConst 'ENU=Cannot create another parking order or add another parking line, because parking order already exists for this customer.';
            Error001@1007 : TextConst 'ENU=Cannot add another parking order for this until previuos is not closed.';
            Answer@1008 : Boolean;
            Question@1009 : TextConst 'ENU=Parking Order for this car already exists. You need to close it before adding another one. Would you like to close it now?';
            ParkingHeaderNew@1010 : Record 60000;
            PostedParkingOrder@1011 : Page 60008;
          BEGIN
            EnterCarPlateNo.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
            IF EnterCarPlateNo.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
              CarPlateNo := EnterCarPlateNo.ReturnCarPlateNo;
              CLEAR(EnterCarPlateNo);
              ParkingLines.SETFILTER("Entry Time",'<>%1',0DT);
              ParkingLines.SETFILTER("Departure Time",'=%1',0DT);
              ParkingLines.SETRANGE("Car Plate No.",CarPlateNo);
              IF NOT ParkingLines.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                Cars.SETRANGE("Car Plate No.",CarPlateNo);
                IF Cars.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                 ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("Customer No.",Cars."Customer No.");
                 IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                   IF ParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" = TRUE THEN BEGIN
                    ParkingLines.RESET;
                    ParkingLines.INIT;
                    ParkingLines."Parking Order No." := ParkingHeader."No.";
                    ParkingLines."Entry Time" := CURRENTDATETIME;
                    ParkingLines.VALIDATE("Car Plate No.",CarPlateNo);
                    IF ParkingLines.INSERT(TRUE) THEN BEGIN
                     ParkingOrder.SETRECORD(ParkingHeader);
                     ParkingOrder.RUN;
                    END;
                   END ELSE BEGIN
                    ERROR(Error000);
                   END;
                 END ELSE BEGIN
                  ParkingHeader.INIT;
                  IF ParkingHeader.INSERT(TRUE) THEN BEGIN
                   ParkingLines.RESET;
                   ParkingLines.SETRANGE("Parking Order No.",ParkingHeader."No.");
                   IF ParkingLines.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                    ParkingLines.VALIDATE("Car Plate No.",CarPlateNo);
                    ParkingLines.MODIFY;
                   END;
                   ParkingOrder.SETRECORD(ParkingHeader);
                   ParkingOrder.RUN;
                  END;
                 END;
                END ELSE BEGIN
                 ParkingHeader.RESET;
                 ParkingLines.RESET;
                 ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("Customer No.",'A00008');
                 IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                  REPEAT
                  ParkingLines.SETRANGE("Parking Order No.",ParkingHeader."No.");
                  IF ParkingLines.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                   REPEAT
                   IF ParkingLines."Car Plate No." = CarPlateNo THEN BEGIN
                    Answer := DIALOG.CONFIRM(Question,FALSE);
                    IF Answer = TRUE THEN BEGIN
                     ParkingOrder.SETRECORD(ParkingHeader);
                     ParkingOrder.RUN;
                     BREAK;
                     EXIT;
                    END ELSE BEGIN
                      EXIT;
                    END;
                   END;
                   UNTIL ParkingLines.NEXT <=0;
                  END;
                  UNTIL ParkingHeader.NEXT <= 0;
                  IF Answer = FALSE THEN BEGIN
                   //ParkingHeader.RESET;
                   ParkingHeaderNew.INIT;
                   IF ParkingHeaderNew.INSERT(TRUE) THEN BEGIN
                    ParkingLines.RESET;
                    ParkingLines.SETRANGE("Parking Order No.",ParkingHeaderNew."No.");
                    IF ParkingLines.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                     ParkingLines.VALIDATE("Car Plate No.",CarPlateNo);
                     ParkingLines.MODIFY;
                    END;
                    ParkingOrder.SETRECORD(ParkingHeaderNew);
                    ParkingOrder.RUN;
                   END;
                  END;
                 END ELSE BEGIN
                  ParkingHeaderNew.INIT;
                  IF ParkingHeaderNew.INSERT(TRUE) THEN BEGIN
                   ParkingLines.RESET;
                   ParkingLines.SETRANGE("Parking Order No.",ParkingHeaderNew."No.");
                   IF ParkingLines.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                    ParkingLines.VALIDATE("Car Plate No.",CarPlateNo);
                    ParkingLines.MODIFY;
                   END;
                   ParkingOrder.SETRECORD(ParkingHeaderNew);
                   ParkingOrder.RUN;
                  END;
                 END;
                END;
              END ELSE BEGIN
                ParkingHeaderNew.SETRANGE("No.", ParkingLines."Parking Order No.");
                IF ParkingHeaderNew.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                  IF NOT ParkingHeaderNew."Accumulative Account" = TRUE THEN BEGIN
                   Answer := DIALOG.CONFIRM(Question,FALSE);
                   IF Answer = TRUE THEN BEGIN
                    ParkingLines.VALIDATE("Departure Time",CURRENTDATETIME);
                    ParkingLines.MODIFY;
                    ParkingOrder.SETRECORD(ParkingHeaderNew);
                    ParkingOrder.PageCheckPosting;
                    ParkingOrder.PagePosting;
                    EXIT;
                   END ELSE BEGIN
                    EXIT;
                   END;
                  END ELSE BEGIN
                    ParkingLines.VALIDATE("Departure Time",CURRENTDATETIME);
                    ParkingLines.MODIFY;
                  END;
                END;
              END;
            END;
          END;

  }
  CODE
  {
    VAR
      EnterCarPlateNo@1000 : Page 60022;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }
}
