OBJECT Page 60000 Parking Order
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=22-03-02;
    Time=12:01:15;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    SourceTable=Table60000;
    UsageCategory=Documents;
    OnNewRecord=VAR
                  Error01@1001 : TextConst 'ENU=Parking lot is full';
                BEGIN
                END;

    ActionList=ACTIONS
    {
      { 19      ;    ;ActionContainer;
                      CaptionML=ENU=General;
                      ActionContainerType=NewDocumentItems }
      { 21      ;1   ;Action    ;
                      Name=Post;
                      OnAction=VAR
                                 Message002@1000 : TextConst 'ENU=You need to check parking order before posting it.';
                                 PostedParkingOrderId@1003 : Code[20];
                                 PostedParkingHeader@1002 : Record 60008;
                                 PostedParkingOrder@1001 : Page 60008;
                               BEGIN
                                 IF "Posting Date" = 0DT THEN
                                  "Posting Date" := CURRENTDATETIME;
                                 Check := FALSE;
                                 Check := ParkingOrderPost.CheckOrder(Rec);
                                 MODIFY;

                                 IF Check = TRUE THEN BEGIN
                                  PostedParkingOrderId := ParkingOrderPost.PostOrder(Rec);
                                  Check := FALSE;
                                  PostedParkingHeader.SETRANGE("No.",PostedParkingOrderId);
                                  IF PostedParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                   IF (PostedParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" = FALSE) AND (PostedParkingHeader.Contract = FALSE) THEN BEGIN
                                    PostedParkingOrder.SETRECORD(PostedParkingHeader);
                                    //PostedParkingOrder.MakeAPayment;
                                    PostedParkingOrder.RUN;
                                   END;
                                  END;
                                 END;
                               END;
                                }
      { 13      ;1   ;Action    ;
                      Name=Find order;
                      OnAction=VAR
                                 CarPlateNo@1000 : Code[20];
                                 Cars@1001 : Record 60003;
                                 ParkingLines@1002 : Record 60001;
                                 Text000@1003 : TextConst 'ENU=Cannot found this car in parking lot';
                                 ParkingHeader@1004 : Record 60000;
                               BEGIN
                                 EnterCarplateNo.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
                                 IF EnterCarplateNo.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
                                  CarPlateNo := EnterCarplateNo.ReturnCarPlateNo;
                                  CLEAR(EnterCarplateNo);
                                  ParkingLines.SETRANGE("Car Plate No.",CarPlateNo);
                                  //ParkingLines.SETFILTER("Departure Time",'=%1',0DT);
                                  IF ParkingLines.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                   ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("No.",ParkingLines."Parking Order No.");
                                   IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                    CurrPage.SETTABLEVIEW(ParkingHeader);
                                    CurrPage.UPDATE;
                                   END;
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                     MESSAGE(Text000);
                                  END;
                                 END;
                               END;
                                }
    }
  }
  CONTROLS
  {
    { 1   ;    ;Container ;
                Name=General;
                CaptionML=ENU=General;
                ContainerType=ContentArea }

    { 2   ;1   ;Group     ;
                GroupType=Group }

    { 3   ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="No." }

    { 4   ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Customer No." }

    { 5   ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Issued By" }

    { 6   ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Total Amount" }

    { 7   ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Total No. of Entries" }

    { 8   ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Document Date" }

    { 9   ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Posting Date" }

    { 10  ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Customer Name" }

    { 11  ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr=Adress }

    { 12  ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Adress 2" }

    { 14  ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Post Code" }

    { 15  ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr=City }

    { 16  ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr=Contract }

    { 17  ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Accumulative Account" }

    { 25  ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Customer Email" }

    { 24  ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Customer Phone No." }

    { 18  ;1   ;Part      ;
                SubPageLink=Parking Order No.=FIELD(No.);
                PagePartID=Page60001;
                PartType=Page }

  }
  CODE
  {
    VAR
      Check@1000 : Boolean;
      ParkingOrderPost@1001 : Codeunit 60000;
      EnterCarplateNo@1002 : Page 60022;

    PROCEDURE PagePosting@1();
    VAR
      PostedParkingOrder@1000 : Page 60008;
      PostedParkingOrderId@1001 : Code[20];
      PostedParkingHeader@1002 : Record 60008;
    BEGIN
      IF Check = TRUE THEN BEGIN
       PostedParkingOrderId := ParkingOrderPost.PostOrder(Rec);
       Check := FALSE;
      END;
      PostedParkingHeader.SETRANGE("No.",PostedParkingOrderId);
      IF PostedParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        IF (PostedParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" = FALSE) AND (PostedParkingHeader.Contract = FALSE) THEN BEGIN
         PostedParkingOrder.SETRECORD(PostedParkingHeader);
         PostedParkingOrder.MakeAPayment;
         PostedParkingOrder.RUN;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE PageCheckPosting@2();
    VAR
      ParkingOrderPass@1001 : TextConst 'ENU=Parking Order can be posted';
      ParkingOrderFail@1000 : TextConst 'ENU=Parking Order cannot be posted';
    BEGIN
      IF "Posting Date" = 0DT THEN
       "Posting Date" := CURRENTDATETIME;
      Check := FALSE;
      Check := ParkingOrderPost.CheckOrder(Rec);
      //MESSAGE(ParkingOrderPass);
      MODIFY;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }
}

OBJECT Page 60002 Parking Order List
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=22-03-02;
    Time=12:01:03;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    SourceTable=Table60000;
    PageType=List;
    CardPageID=Parking Order;
    ActionList=ACTIONS
    {
      { 17      ;    ;ActionContainer;
                      CaptionML=ENU=General;
                      ActionContainerType=NewDocumentItems }
      { 18      ;1   ;Action    ;
                      Name=Find order;
                      OnAction=VAR
                                 CarPlateNo@1000 : Code[20];
                                 Cars@1001 : Record 60003;
                                 ParkingLines@1002 : Record 60001;
                                 Text000@1003 : TextConst 'ENU=Cannot found this car in parking lot';
                                 ParkingHeader@1004 : Record 60000;
                               BEGIN
                                 EnterCarplateNo.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
                                 IF EnterCarplateNo.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
                                  CarPlateNo := EnterCarplateNo.ReturnCarPlateNo;
                                  CLEAR(EnterCarplateNo);
                                  ParkingLines.SETRANGE("Car Plate No.",CarPlateNo);
                                  //ParkingLines.SETFILTER("Departure Time",'=%1',0DT);
                                  IF ParkingLines.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                   ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("No.",ParkingLines."Parking Order No.");
                                   IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                    CurrPage.SETTABLEVIEW(ParkingHeader);
                                    CurrPage.UPDATE;
                                   END;
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                     MESSAGE(Text000);
                                  END;
                                 END;
                               END;
                                }
      { 20      ;1   ;Action    ;
                      Name=Post;
                      OnAction=VAR
                                 Message002@1000 : TextConst 'ENU=You need to check parking order before posting it.';
                                 PostedParkingOrderId@1003 : Code[20];
                                 PostedParkingHeader@1002 : Record 60008;
                                 PostedParkingOrder@1001 : Page 60008;
                               BEGIN
                                 IF "Posting Date" = 0DT THEN
                                  "Posting Date" := CURRENTDATETIME;
                                 Check := FALSE;
                                 Check := ParkingOrderPost.CheckOrder(Rec);
                                 MODIFY;

                                 IF Check = TRUE THEN BEGIN
                                  PostedParkingOrderId := ParkingOrderPost.PostOrder(Rec);
                                  Check := FALSE;
                                  PostedParkingHeader.SETRANGE("No.",PostedParkingOrderId);
                                  IF PostedParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                   IF (PostedParkingHeader."Accumulative Account" = FALSE) AND (PostedParkingHeader.Contract = FALSE) THEN BEGIN
                                    PostedParkingOrder.SETRECORD(PostedParkingHeader);
                                    //PostedParkingOrder.MakeAPayment;
                                    PostedParkingOrder.RUN;
                                   END;
                                  END;
                                 END;
                               END;
                                }
    }
  }

OBJECT Page 60006 Contracts List
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=22-03-01;
    Time=16:42:03;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    SourceTable=Table60006;
    PageType=List;
    UsageCategory=Documents;
    CardPageID=Contracts Page;
    ActionList=ACTIONS
    {
      { 11      ;    ;ActionContainer;
                      Name=General;
                      ActionContainerType=NewDocumentItems }
      { 12      ;1   ;Action    ;
                      Name=Pay for contract;
                      Promoted=Yes;
                      PromotedIsBig=Yes;
                      Image=Apply;
                      PromotedCategory=Process;
                      PromotedOnly=Yes;
                      OnAction=VAR
                                 PaymentSum@1000 : Decimal;
                                 Error01@1001 : TextConst 'ENU=Contract is already paid';
                                 ContractPayment@1002 : Codeunit 60002;
                                 Customer@1003 : Record 18;
                                 ParkingHeader@1004 : Record 60000;
                                 Date@1008 : Date;
                                 Time@1007 : Time;
                                 NewDateTime@1006 : DateTime;
                                 MyRec@1005 : Record 60006;
                               BEGIN
                                 IF "Remaining Amount" > 0 THEN BEGIN
                                  ConfirmDialog.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
                                  IF ConfirmDialog.RUNMODAL = ACTION::Yes THEN BEGIN
                                   PaymentSum := "Remaining Amount";
                                   CLEAR(ConfirmDialog);
                                   ContractPayment.PostContractPayment(Rec,PaymentSum);
                                   {
                                   Customer.SETRANGE("No.","Customer No.");
                                   IF Customer.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                    Customer.Contract := TRUE;
                                    Customer.MODIFY;
                                   END;
                                   ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("Customer No.",Rec."Customer No.");
                                   IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                    ParkingHeader.Contract := TRUE;
                                    ParkingHeader.MODIFY;
                                   END;
                                   }
                                   CurrPage.UPDATE;
                                  END;
                                  CLEAR(ConfirmDialog);
                                 END ELSE BEGIN
                                  IF ("Remaining Amount" = 0) AND ("Contract End Date" <> 0DT) THEN BEGIN
                                   ExtendContract.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
                                   IF ExtendContract.RUNMODAL = ACTION::Yes THEN BEGIN
                                    PaymentSum := 60;
                                    CLEAR(ExtendContract);
                                    ContractPayment.PostExtendedContract(Rec,PaymentSum);
                                    //ContractPayment.ExtendContract(Rec,PaymentSum);
                                    {
                                    Time := DT2TIME("Contract End Date");
                                    Date := DT2DATE("Contract End Date");
                                    Date += 30;
                                    NewDateTime := CREATEDATETIME(Date,Time);
                                    "Contract End Date" := NewDateTime;
                                    }
                                    {
                                    Customer.SETRANGE("No.","Customer No.");
                                    IF Customer.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                     Customer.Contract := TRUE;
                                     Customer.MODIFY;
                                    END;
                                    }
                                    //CurrPage.UPDATE;
                                   END;
                                   CLEAR(ExtendContract);
                                  END;
                                  CLEAR(ExtendContract);
                                 END;
                                 {
                                 MyRec.SETRANGE("Contract No.",Rec."Contract No.");
                                 MyRec.SETRANGE("Customer No.",Rec."Customer No.");
                                 REPORT.RUNMODAL(60003,FALSE,FALSE,MyRec);
                                 "Remaining Amount" := "Remaining Amount" - PaymentSum;
                                 }
                               END;
                                }
      { 13      ;1   ;Action    ;
                      Name=Filter active contracts;
                      Promoted=Yes;
                      PromotedIsBig=Yes;
                      Image=Apply;
                      PromotedCategory=Process;
                      PromotedOnly=Yes;
                      OnAction=VAR
                                 Contracts@1000 : Record 60006;
                                 ContractList@1001 : Page 60006;
                                 Message000@1002 : TextConst 'ENU=No active contracts founded';
                               BEGIN
                                 Contracts.SETFILTER("Contract End Date",'>%1',CURRENTDATETIME);
                                 IF Contracts.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                   CurrPage.SETTABLEVIEW(Contracts);
                                   CurrPage.UPDATE;
                                 END ELSE BEGIN
                                   MESSAGE(Message000);
                                 END;
                               END;
                                }
      { 14      ;1   ;Action    ;
                      Name=Search contract;
                      Promoted=Yes;
                      PromotedIsBig=Yes;
                      Image=Apply;
                      PromotedCategory=Process;
                      PromotedOnly=Yes;
                      OnAction=VAR
                                 Cars@1000 : Record 60003;
                                 CarPlateNo@1001 : Code[20];
                                 Contracts@1002 : Record 60006;
                                 Message001@1003 : TextConst 'ENU=There are no contracts created for this customer';
                               BEGIN
                                 EnterCarPlateNo.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
                                 IF EnterCarPlateNo.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
                                  CarPlateNo := EnterCarPlateNo.ReturnCarPlateNo;
                                  CLEAR(EnterCarPlateNo);
                                  Cars.SETRANGE("Car Plate No.",CarPlateNo);
                                  IF Cars.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                    Contracts.SETRANGE("Customer No.",Cars."Customer No.");
                                    IF Contracts.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                     CurrPage.SETTABLEVIEW(Contracts);
                                     CurrPage.UPDATE;
                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                     MESSAGE(Message001);
                                    END;
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                  MESSAGE(Message001);
                                  END;
                                 END;
                               END;
                                }
    }
  }
  CONTROLS
  {
    { 1   ;0   ;Container ;
                ContainerType=ContentArea }

    { 2   ;1   ;Group     ;
                Name=Group;
                GroupType=Repeater }

    { 3   ;2   ;Field     ;

    PROCEDURE MakeAPayment@1();
    BEGIN
      Rec.CALCFIELDS("Remaining Amount");
      IF "Remaining Amount" > 0 THEN BEGIN
       PaymentPost.PostPayment(Rec,"Remaining Amount");
       CurrPage.UPDATE;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        ERROR(Error01);
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

OBJECT Page 60020 Parked cars List
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=22-02-17;
    Time=11:11:16;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    Editable=No;
    SourceTable=Table60001;
    SourceTableView=SORTING(Parking Order No.,Line No.)
                    WHERE(Departure Time=FILTER(=''),
                          Entry Time=FILTER(<>''));
    PageType=ListPart;
    OnOpenPage=VAR
                 UserSetup@1000 : Record 91;
               BEGIN
                 UserSetup.GET(USERID);
                 IF (UserSetup."User ID" <> 'ADMIN') OR (UserSetup."User ID" <> 'ADMINISTRATOR') THEN
                  SETFILTER("Parking Lot No.",UserSetup."Parking Lot No.");
               END;

    OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                       NewDateTime := CREATEDATETIME(TODAY,TIME);
                       ParkingDuration := ROUND(NewDateTime - "Entry Time", 1000 * 60);
                     END;

    ActionList=ACTIONS
    {
      { 7       ;    ;ActionContainer;
                      CaptionML=ENU=General;
                      ActionContainerType=ActionItems }
      { 11      ;1   ;Action    ;
                      Name=Find Car Order;
                      Promoted=Yes;
                      PromotedIsBig=Yes;
                      Image=Apply;
                      PromotedCategory=Process;
                      PromotedOnly=Yes;
                      OnAction=VAR
                                 Cars@1000 : Record 60003;
                                 CarPlateNo@1001 : Code[20];
                                 ParkingLines@1002 : Record 60001;
                                 ParkingOrder@1003 : Page 60000;
                                 ParkingHeader@1004 : Record 60000;
                               BEGIN
                                 EnterCarPlateNo.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
                                 IF EnterCarPlateNo.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
                                  CarPlateNo := EnterCarPlateNo.ReturnCarPlateNo;
                                  CLEAR(EnterCarPlateNo);
                                  ParkingLines.COPYFILTERS(Rec);
                                  ParkingLines.SETRANGE("Car Plate No.",CarPlateNo);
                                  IF ParkingLines.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                    ParkingHeader.GET(ParkingLines."Parking Order No.");
                                    ParkingOrder.SETRECORD(ParkingHeader);
                                    ParkingOrder.RUN;
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                   MESSAGE('There is no car');
                                  END;
                                 END;
                               END;
                                }
    }
  }
  CONTROLS
  {
    { 1   ;0   ;Container ;
                ContainerType=ContentArea }

    { 2   ;1   ;Group     ;
                Name=Group;
                GroupType=Repeater }

    { 5   ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Entry Time" }

    { 6   ;2   ;Field     ;
                Name=<ParkingDuration>;
                CaptionML=ENU=ParkingDuration;
                SourceExpr=ParkingDuration }

    { 8   ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Car Plate No." }

    { 10  ;2   ;Field     ;
                SourceExpr="Parking Lot No." }

  }
  CODE
  {
    VAR
      ParkingDuration@1002 : Duration;
      NewDateTime@1001 : DateTime;
      EnterCarPlateNo@1000 : Page 60022;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }
}

      { 22      ;1   ;Action    ;
                      Name=Clients, who needs to pay;
                      OnAction=VAR
                                 PostedParkingHeader@1000 : Record 60008;
                                 Message001@1001 : TextConst 'ENU=No records found';
                               BEGIN
                                 PostedParkingHeader.SETFILTER("Remaining Amount",'>%1',0);
                                 IF PostedParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                  CurrPage.SETTABLEVIEW(PostedParkingHeader);
                                  CurrPage.UPDATE;
                                 END ELSE BEGIN
                                  MESSAGE(Message001);
                                 END;
                               END;

      { 24      ;1   ;Action    ;
                      Name=Make a payment;
                      OnAction=VAR
                                 PaymentPost@1001 : Codeunit 60001;
                                 Error01@1002 : TextConst 'ENU=Payment is already done';
                               BEGIN
                                 IF "Remaining Amount" > 0 THEN BEGIN
                                  ConfirmDialog.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
                                  IF ConfirmDialog.RUNMODAL = ACTION::Yes THEN BEGIN
                                   //PaymentSum := "Remaining Amount";
                                   CLEAR(ConfirmDialog);
                                   PaymentPost.PostPayment(Rec,"Remaining Amount");
                                   CurrPage.UPDATE;
                                  END;
                                 END ELSE BEGIN
                                   ERROR(Error01);
                                 END;
                               END;
                                }
      { 25      ;1   ;Action    ;
                      Name=Cheque for accumulative account;
                      OnAction=VAR
                                 MyRec@1000 : Record 60008;
                                 Message002@1001 : TextConst 'ENU=This is not a accumulative account';
                               BEGIN
                                 IF Rec."Accumulative Account" = TRUE THEN BEGIN
                                  MyRec.SETRANGE("No.",Rec."No.");
                                  REPORT.RUNMODAL(60006,FALSE,FALSE,MyRec);
                                 END ELSE BEGIN
                                  MESSAGE(Message002);
                                 END;
                               END;
                                }
    }
  }

OBJECT Page 60025 Watchman Customers
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=22-02-09;
    Time=11:50:06;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=NAVW114.00;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=ENU=My Customers;
    SourceTable=Table9150;
    PageType=ListPart;
    OnOpenPage=BEGIN
                 SETRANGE("User ID",USERID);
               END;

    OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                       SyncFieldsWithCustomer;
                     END;

    OnNewRecord=BEGIN
                  CLEAR(Customer)
                END;

    ActionList=ACTIONS
    {
      { 1900000004;0 ;ActionContainer;
                      ActionContainerType=ActionItems }
      { 2       ;1   ;Action    ;
                      ShortCutKey=Return;
                      CaptionML=ENU=Open;
                      ToolTipML=ENU=Open the card for the selected record.;
                      ApplicationArea=#Basic,#Suite;
                      RunObject=Page 21;
                      RunPageView=SORTING(No.);
                      RunPageLink=No.=FIELD(Customer No.);
                      Image=ViewDetails;
                      RunPageMode=View;
                      Scope=Repeater }
    }
  }
  CONTROLS
  {
    { 1900000001;0;Container;
                ContainerType=ContentArea }

    { 1   ;1   ;Group     ;
                GroupType=Repeater }

    { 4   ;2   ;Field     ;
                Width=4;
                ToolTipML=ENU=Specifies the customer numbers that are displayed in the My Customer Cue on the Role Center.;
                ApplicationArea=#Basic,#Suite;
                SourceExpr="Customer No.";
                OnValidate=BEGIN
                             SyncFieldsWithCustomer;
                           END;
                            }

    { 9   ;2   ;Field     ;
                Width=20;
                Lookup=No;
                DrillDown=No;
                CaptionML=ENU=Name;
                ToolTipML=ENU=Specifies the name of the customer.;
                ApplicationArea=#Basic,#Suite;
                SourceExpr=Name }

    { 11  ;2   ;Field     ;
                ExtendedDatatype=Phone No.;
                Width=8;
                Lookup=No;
                DrillDown=No;
                CaptionML=ENU=Phone No.;
                ToolTipML=ENU=Specifies the customer's phone number.;
                ApplicationArea=#Basic,#Suite;
                SourceExpr="Phone No." }

    { 3   ;2   ;Field     ;
                ToolTipML=ENU=Specifies the payment amount that the customer owes for completed sales.;
                ApplicationArea=#Basic,#Suite;
                SourceExpr="Balance (LCY)";
                OnDrillDown=BEGIN
                              Customer.OpenCustomerLedgerEntries(FALSE);
                            END;
                             }

  }
  CODE
  {
    VAR
      Customer@1000 : Record 18;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SyncFieldsWithCustomer@2();
    VAR
      MyCustomer@1000 : Record 9150;
    BEGIN
      CLEAR(Customer);

      IF Customer.GET("Customer No.") THEN
        IF (Name <> Customer.Name) OR ("Phone No." <> Customer."Phone No.") THEN BEGIN
          Name := Customer.Name;
          "Phone No." := Customer."Phone No.";
          IF MyCustomer.GET("User ID","Customer No.") THEN
            MODIFY;
        END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }
}

OBJECT Page 60027 Parking Lot summary
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=22-04-29;
    Time=22:28:10;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=NAVW114.18;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=ENU=Parking lot summary;
    SourceTable=Table60012;
    PageType=CardPart;
    RefreshOnActivate=Yes;
    OnOpenPage=VAR
                 RoleCenterNotificationMgt@1000 : Codeunit 1430;
                 ConfPersonalizationMgt@1001 : Codeunit 9170;
                 UserSetup@1002 : Record 91;
               BEGIN
                 RESET;
                 IF NOT GET THEN BEGIN
                   INIT;
                   INSERT;
                 END;


                 UserSetup.GET(USERID);
                 IF UserSetup."User ID" = 'WATCHMAN1' THEN
                  ParkingLot2Hidden := TRUE;
                 IF UserSetup."User ID" = 'WATCHMAN2' THEN
                  ParkingLot1Hidden := TRUE;

               END;

    OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                       DocExchServiceSetup@1000 : Record 1275;
                       Contracts@1001 : Record 60006;
                     BEGIN
                       CalculateCueFieldValues;
                       ShowDocumentsPendingDodExchService := FALSE;
                       IF DocExchServiceSetup.GET THEN
                         ShowDocumentsPendingDodExchService := DocExchServiceSetup.Enabled;

                       Contracts.SETFILTER("Contract End Date",'>%1',CURRENTDATETIME);
                       IF Contracts.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                         REPEAT
                           ActiveContracts := ActiveContracts + 1;
                         UNTIL Contracts.NEXT = 0;
                       END;

                       Contracts.RESET;

                       Contracts.SETFILTER("Contract End Date",'<%1',CURRENTDATETIME);
                       IF Contracts.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                         REPEAT
                           EndedContracts := EndedContracts + 1;
                         UNTIL Contracts.NEXT = 0;
                       END;
                       "Active contracts" := ActiveContracts;
                       "Ended contracts" := EndedContracts;
                       EndedContracts := 0;
                       ActiveContracts := 0;
                       CurrPage.UPDATE;
                     END;

    OnAfterGetCurrRecord=VAR
                           RoleCenterNotificationMgt@1000 : Codeunit 1430;
                         BEGIN
                           RoleCenterNotificationMgt.HideEvaluationNotificationAfterStartingTrial;
                         END;

    ActionList=ACTIONS
    {
      { 5       ;    ;ActionContainer;
                      ActionContainerType=ActionItems }
    }
  }
  CONTROLS
  {
    { 1900000001;0;Container;
                ContainerType=ContentArea }

    { 1   ;1   ;Group     ;
                CaptionML=ENU=Parking Lot;
                GroupType=CueGroup;
                Layout=Wide;
                ActionList=ACTIONS
                {
                  { 2       ;    ;Action    ;
                                  Name=<Contracts>;
                                  CaptionML=ENU=New Contract;
                                  RunObject=Page 60028;
                                  RunPageMode=Create }
                  { 3       ;    ;Action    ;
                                  Name=<Accumulative Contract>;
                                  CaptionML=ENU=New Accumulative Contract;
                                  RunObject=Page 60017;
                                  RunPageMode=Create }
                  { 9       ;    ;Action    ;
                                  Name=<Register cars>;
                                  CaptionML=ENU=Register Cars;
                                  RunObject=Page 60016;
                                  RunPageMode=Create }

OBJECT Page 60028 Contracts Page
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=22-03-01;
    Time=16:42:26;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    SourceTable=Table60006;
    ActionList=ACTIONS
    {
      { 11      ;    ;ActionContainer;
                      CaptionML=ENU=General;
                      ActionContainerType=NewDocumentItems }
      { 13      ;1   ;Action    ;
                      Name=Pay for contract;
                      Promoted=Yes;
                      PromotedIsBig=Yes;
                      Image=Apply;
                      PromotedCategory=Process;
                      PromotedOnly=Yes;
                      OnAction=VAR
                                 PaymentSum@1000 : Decimal;
                                 Error01@1001 : TextConst 'ENU=Contract is already paid';
                                 ContractPayment@1002 : Codeunit 60002;
                                 Customer@1003 : Record 18;
                                 ParkingHeader@1004 : Record 60000;
                                 Date@1008 : Date;
                                 Time@1007 : Time;
                                 NewDateTime@1006 : DateTime;
                                 MyRec@1005 : Record 60006;
                               BEGIN
                                 IF "Remaining Amount" > 0 THEN BEGIN
                                  ConfirmDialog.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
                                  IF ConfirmDialog.RUNMODAL = ACTION::Yes THEN BEGIN
                                   PaymentSum := "Remaining Amount";
                                   CLEAR(ConfirmDialog);
                                   ContractPayment.PostContractPayment(Rec,PaymentSum);
                                   {
                                   Customer.SETRANGE("No.","Customer No.");
                                   IF Customer.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                    Customer.Contract := TRUE;
                                    Customer.MODIFY;
                                   END;
                                   ParkingHeader.SETRANGE("Customer No.",Rec."Customer No.");
                                   IF ParkingHeader.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                    ParkingHeader.Contract := TRUE;
                                    ParkingHeader.MODIFY;
                                   END;
                                   }
                                   CurrPage.UPDATE;
                                  END;
                                  CLEAR(ConfirmDialog);
                                 END ELSE BEGIN
                                  IF ("Remaining Amount" = 0) AND ("Contract End Date" <> 0DT) THEN BEGIN
                                   ExtendContract.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
                                   IF ExtendContract.RUNMODAL = ACTION::Yes THEN BEGIN
                                    PaymentSum := 60;
                                    CLEAR(ExtendContract);
                                    ContractPayment.PostExtendedContract(Rec,PaymentSum);
                                    //ContractPayment.ExtendContract(Rec,PaymentSum);
                                    {
                                    Time := DT2TIME("Contract End Date");
                                    Date := DT2DATE("Contract End Date");
                                    Date += 30;
                                    NewDateTime := CREATEDATETIME(Date,Time);
                                    "Contract End Date" := NewDateTime;
                                    }
                                    {
                                    Customer.SETRANGE("No.","Customer No.");
                                    IF Customer.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                     Customer.Contract := TRUE;
                                     Customer.MODIFY;
                                    END;
                                    }
                                    //CurrPage.UPDATE;
                                   END;
                                   CLEAR(ExtendContract);
                                  END;
                                  CLEAR(ExtendContract);
                                 END;
                                 {
                                 MyRec.SETRANGE("Contract No.",Rec."Contract No.");
                                 MyRec.SETRANGE("Customer No.",Rec."Customer No.");
                                 REPORT.RUNMODAL(60003,FALSE,FALSE,MyRec);
                                 "Remaining Amount" := "Remaining Amount" - PaymentSum;
                                 }
                               END;
                                }
      { 12      ;1   ;Action    ;
                      Name=Search contract;
                      Promoted=Yes;
                      PromotedIsBig=Yes;
                      Image=Apply;
                      PromotedCategory=Process;
                      PromotedOnly=Yes;
                      OnAction=VAR
                                 Cars@1000 : Record 60003;
                                 CarPlateNo@1001 : Code[20];
                                 Contracts@1002 : Record 60006;
                                 Message000@1003 : TextConst 'ENU=There are no contracts created for this customer';
                               BEGIN
                                 EnterCarPlateNo.LOOKUPMODE(TRUE);
                                 IF EnterCarPlateNo.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
                                  CarPlateNo := EnterCarPlateNo.ReturnCarPlateNo;
                                  CLEAR(EnterCarPlateNo);
                                  Cars.SETRANGE("Car Plate No.",CarPlateNo);
                                  IF Cars.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                    Contracts.SETRANGE("Customer No.",Cars."Customer No.");
                                    IF Contracts.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                     CurrPage.SETTABLEVIEW(Contracts);
                                     CurrPage.UPDATE;
                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                     MESSAGE(Message000);
                                    END;
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                  MESSAGE(Message000);
                                  END;
                                 END;
                               END;
                                }
    }
  }
  CONTROLS
  {
    { 1   ;    ;Container ;
                CaptionML=ENU=General;
                ContainerType=ContentArea }

    { 10  ;1   ;Group     ;
                GroupType=Group }

    { 2   ;2   ;Field     ;

               BEGIN

                   INIT;

                 IF UserSetup."User ID" = 'WATCHMAN2' THEN
                  ParkingLot1Hidden := TRUE;

                       DocExchServiceSetup@1000 : Record 1275;
                       Contracts@1001 : Record 60006;
                     BEGIN
                       CalculateCueFieldValues;
                       ShowDocumentsPendingDodExchService := FALSE;
                       IF DocExchServiceSetup.GET THEN
                         ShowDocumentsPendingDodExchService := DocExchServiceSetup.Enabled;

                       Contracts.SETFILTER("Contract End Date",'>%1',CURRENTDATETIME);
                       IF Contracts.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                         REPEAT
                           ActiveContracts := ActiveContracts + 1;
                         UNTIL Contracts.NEXT = 0;
                       END;

                       Contracts.RESET;

                       Contracts.SETFILTER("Contract End Date",'<%1',CURRENTDATETIME);
                       IF Contracts.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                         REPEAT
                           EndedContracts := EndedContracts + 1;
                         UNTIL Contracts.NEXT = 0;
                       END;
                       "Active contracts" := ActiveContracts;
                       "Ended contracts" := EndedContracts;
                       EndedContracts := 0;
                       ActiveContracts := 0;
                       CurrPage.UPDATE;
                     END;

    OnAfterGetCurrRecord=VAR
                           RoleCenterNotificationMgt@1000 : Codeunit 1430;
                         BEGIN
                           RoleCenterNotificationMgt.HideEvaluationNotificationAfterStartingTrial;
                         END;
